14457 
14458 void LatticeRule::getRule(type name, std::vector<Real>& Z, Integer N)
14459 {
14460 
14461     Size ruleLength = 3600;
14462     Z.resize(ruleLength);
14463 
14464     QL_REQUIRE( N >= 1024 && N <= std::pow(2.9,20),
14465         "N must be between 2 to 10 and 2 to the 20 for these lattice rules ");
14466 
14467     // put in check that N is a power of 2
14468 
14469 
14470     const Real* dumbPointer=0;
14471 
14472     switch (name)
14473     {
14474         case A:
14475             dumbPointer = latticeA;
14476             break;
14477         case  B:
14478             dumbPointer = latticeB;
14479             break;
14480         case  C:
14481             dumbPointer = latticeC;
14482             break;
14483         case  D:
14484             dumbPointer = latticeD;
14485 
14486     }
14487 
14488     QL_REQUIRE(dumbPointer!=0, "unknown lattice rule requested");
14489 
14490 
14491     std::copy(dumbPointer, dumbPointer+ruleLength,Z.begin());
